### MODDER: DK and esmaerla ###
### Ausgleich Events ###

add_namespace = ausgleich

### Trigger 
news_event = {
	id = ausgleich.1
	title = ausgleich.1.t
	desc = ausgleich.1.d
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		country_exists = AUS
		date > 1937.2.1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		AUS = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.2 }}
		set_global_flag = ausgleich_37
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.1.a
	}
}

### Ausgleich Event for Austria

### Decides what course to take
country_event = {
	id = ausgleich.2
	title = ausgleich.2.t
	desc = ausgleich.2.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.2.a #Stay Dualism

		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }

		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = austria_dualism
			}

			add_opinion_modifier = { modifier = dualism_disagree }
		}

		GER = { add_opinion_modifier = {target = AUS modifier = dualism_agree} }
		add_opinion_modifier = {target = GER modifier = dualism_agree}

		HUN = {country_event = { id = ausgleich.3 days = 1 }}	
	}

	option = {
		name = ausgleich.2.b #Federalism

		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }

		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = austria_dualism
			}

			add_opinion_modifier = { modifier = federalism_agree }
		}

		GER = { add_opinion_modifier = {target = AUS modifier = federlism_disagree}}

		HUN = {country_event = { id = ausgleich.4 days = 1 }}		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.2.c #Centralize

		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }

		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = austria_dualism
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {target = this modifier = centralize_disagree}
		}

		HUN = {country_event = { id = ausgleich.5 days = 1 }}	
	}
}

### Stay dualism
country_event = {
	id = ausgleich.3
	title = ausgleich.3.t
	desc = ausgleich.3.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.3.a # Accept

		ai_chance = { factor = 60 }

		AUS = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.6 days = 1 }}

		add_opinion_modifier = {target = GER modifier = HUN_stay_dualism_GER } # 50
		add_opinion_modifier = {target = BOM modifier = HUN_stay_dualism_EMP } # -30
		add_opinion_modifier = {target = CRO modifier = HUN_stay_dualism_EMP } # -30
		add_opinion_modifier = {target = GAL modifier = HUN_stay_dualism_EMP } # -30
		add_opinion_modifier = {target = BOS modifier = HUN_stay_dualism_EMP } # -30
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.3.b # Decline
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }

		AUS = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.24 days = 3 }}
	}
}

### Become Federation
country_event = {
	id = ausgleich.4
	title = ausgleich.4.t
	desc = ausgleich.4.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.4.a # Accept

		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }

		AUS = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.10 days = 0 }}

		end_puppet = CRO

		add_political_power = -200

		add_opinion_modifier = {target = GER modifier = HUN_federate_GER } # -80
		add_opinion_modifier = {target = BOM modifier = HUN_federate_EMP } # 50
		add_opinion_modifier = {target = CRO modifier = HUN_federate_EMP } # 50
		add_opinion_modifier = {target = GAL modifier = HUN_federate_EMP } # 50
		add_opinion_modifier = {target = BOS modifier = HUN_federate_EMP } # 50	
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.4.b # Decline

		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }

		AUS = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.25 days = 3 }}
	}
}

	desc = ausgleich.6.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {

		country_event = { id = ausgleich.7 days = 1 }
	}
}

country_event = { # Galicia and Poland
	id = ausgleich.7
	title = ausgleich.7.t
	desc = ausgleich.7.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.7.a

		ai_chance = { factor = 70 }

		add_opinion_modifier = { target = HUN modifier = gal_to_poland } # -50

		POL = {country_event = { id = ausgleich.8 days = 3 }}
	}

	option = {
		name = ausgleich.7.b

		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }

		add_opinion_modifier = { target = POL modifier = galitzia_in_empire } # -50
	}
}

country_event = { # An offer from Austria
	id = ausgleich.8
	title = ausgleich.8.t
	desc = ausgleich.8.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.8.a

		ai_chance = { factor = 80 }

		annex_country = { target = GAL transfer_troops = no }

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { is_core_of = GAL }

			add_core_of = POL
		}

		set_country_flag = Galicia_Annexed

		AUS = {country_event = { id = ausgleich.9 days = 3 }}
	}

	option = {
		name = ausgleich.8.b

		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }

		add_opinion_modifier = { target = POL modifier = galitzia_in_empire } # -50
	}
}

country_event = { # Poland has accepted our offer
	id = ausgleich.9
	title = ausgleich.9.t
	desc = ausgleich.9.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.9.a

		puppet = POL
	}
}

### Federalism Agreed
country_event = {
	id = ausgleich.10
	title = ausgleich.10.t
	desc = ausgleich.10.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.10.a

		add_opinion_modifier = { target = HUN modifier = AUS_accepted_federalism } # 100

		puppet = CRO

		BOM = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.11 days = 0 }}
		CRO = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.11 days = 0 }}
		GAL = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.11 days = 0 }}
		BOS = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.11 days = 0 }}
	}	
}

### Federalisation of the Empire
country_event = {
	id = ausgleich.11
	title = ausgleich.11.t
	desc = ausgleich.11.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.11.a

		hidden_effect = { retire_country_leader = yes }

		if = {
			limit = { tag = BOM }

			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Otto I von Habsburg-Lothringen"
				desc = "POLITICS_OTTO_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_Austria_Otto_I_2.tga"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = social_conservatist_subtype
				traits = { }
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = { tag = CRO }

			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Otto I von Habsburg-Lothringen"
				desc = "POLITICS_OTTO_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_Austria_Otto_I_2.tga"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = authoritarian_democratist_subtype
				traits = { }
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = { tag = GAL }

			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Otto I von Habsburg-Lothringen"
				desc = "POLITICS_OTTO_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_Austria_Otto_I_2.tga"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = paternal_autocratist_subtype
				traits = { }
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = { tag = BOS }

			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Otto I von Habsburg-Lothringen"
				desc = "POLITICS_OTTO_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_Austria_Otto_I_2.tga"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = authoritarian_democratist_subtype
				traits = { }
			}
		}
	}	
}

#Centralisation
###############

### Centralisation Agreed
country_event = {
	id = ausgleich.12
	title = ausgleich.12.t
	desc = ausgleich.12.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.12.a

		add_political_power = -100
		
		AUS = { annex_country = { target = HUN transfer_troops = yes }}

		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = BOM
					is_core_of = CRO
					is_core_of = GAL
					is_core_of = BOS
					is_core_of = HUN
				}
			}

			add_core_of AUS
		}
		
		BOM = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.13 days = 1 }}
		CRO = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.13 days = 1 }}
		GAL = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.13 days = 1 }}
		BOS = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.13 days = 1 }}
		
		AUS = { puppet = CRO}
		
		set_global_flag = centralize_success
	}
}

### Minor States
country_event = {
	id = ausgleich.13
	title = ausgleich.13.t
	desc = ausgleich.13.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.13.a # Accept

		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 100 
			modifier = {
				tag = GAL
				factor = 80
			}
		}


		if ={
			limit = { tag = BOM }

			AUS = { end_puppet = BOM }
			AUS = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.16 days = 1 }}
		}

		if ={
			limit = { tag = CRO }
			
			AUS = { end_puppet = CRO }
			AUS = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.17 days = 1 }}
		}

		if ={
			limit = { tag = GAL }
			
			AUS = { end_puppet = GAL }
			AUS = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.18 days = 1 }}
		}

		if ={
			limit = { tag = BOS }
			
			AUS = { end_puppet = BOS }
			AUS = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.19 days = 1 }}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ausgleich.13.b # Decline

		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }

		if ={
			limit = { tag = BOM }

			AUS = { end_puppet = BOM }
			AUS = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.20 days = 1 }}
		}

		if ={
			limit = { tag = CRO }
			
			AUS = { end_puppet = CRO }
			AUS = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.21 days = 1 }}
		}

		if ={
			limit = { tag = GAL }
			
			AUS = { end_puppet = GAL }
			AUS = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.22 days = 1 }}
		}

		if ={
			limit = { tag = BOS }
			
			AUS = { end_puppet = BOS }
			AUS = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.23 days = 1 }}
		}	
	}

	option = {
		name = ausgleich.13.c # Join Poland

		trigger = {
			tag = GAL
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }

		POL = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.14 days = 1 }}
	}	
}

country_event = { # Galicia wants to join Poland!
	id = ausgleich.14
	title = ausgleich.14.t
	desc = ausgleich.14.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { set_global_flag = galicia_wants_to_join_poland }
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.14.a

		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }

		annex_country = { target = GAL transfer_troops = no }

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { is_core_of = GAL }

			add_core_of = POL
		}

		set_country_flag = Galicia_Annexed

		add_opinion_modifier = { target = AUS modifier = POL_ann_GAL_AUS } # -100
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = HUN modifier = POL_ann_GAL_AUS } # -100
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = POL_ann_GAL_GER } # -50
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = UKR modifier = POL_ann_GAL_GER } # -50
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = WHR modifier = POL_ann_GAL_BLR } # -5

		AUS = {country_event = { id = ausgleich.15 days = 3 }}
	}

	option = {
		name = ausgleich.14.b

		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }

		add_opinion_modifier = { target = AUS modifier = POL_no_ann_GAL_AUS } # 100
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = HUN modifier = POL_no_ann_GAL_AUS } # 100
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = POL_no_ann_GAL_GER } # 50
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = GAL modifier = POL_no_ann_GAL_GAL } # -100

		AUS = {country_event = { id = ausgleich.15 days = 3 }}
	}
}

country_event = { # Galicia joins Poland!
	id = ausgleich.15
	title = ausgleich.15.t
	desc = ausgleich.15.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.15.a

		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }

		declare_war_on = {
			target = POL
			type = take_core_state
			generator = { 88 91 89 80 } 
		}

		add_political_power = -60 
	}

	option = {
		name = ausgleich.15.b

		ai_chance = { factor = 80 }

		add_political_power = -80 

		add_opinion_modifier = { target = POL modifier = POL_ann_GAL_AUS_noth } # 100
	}
}

	}

		name = ausgleich.24.b #decline

		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }

		end_puppet = HUN
		GER = { country_event = {id = ausgleich.31 days = 1 }} # German intervention	
	}
}

	id = ausgleich.28
	title = ausgleich.28.t
	desc = ausgleich.28.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {

	option = {
		name = ausgleich.28.b

		ai_chance = { factor = 60 }

	}

		name = ausgleich.28.c

		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }

			limit = { is_core_of = BOS }

			add_claim_by = HUN
		}	
	}
}

### German intervention
country_event = {
	id = ausgleich.31
	title = ausgleich.31.t
	desc = ausgleich.31.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.31.a # Pro Asutria

		ai_chance = { factor = 35 }

		HUN = {country_event = {id = ausgleich.32 days = 1}}
		
		add_political_power = -100
	}
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.31.b # Pro Hungary

		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }

		AUS = {country_event = {id = ausgleich.34 days = 1}}
		
		add_political_power = -40	
	}
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.31.c # Neutral

		ai_chance = { factor = 35 }

		AUS = {country_event = {id = ausgleich.40 days = 1}}
		
		add_political_power = -100
	}
}

	id = ausgleich.40
	title = ausgleich.40.t
	desc = ausgleich.40.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { 
		HUN = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.41 days = 0 }} 
		declare_war_on = { target = HUN type = annex_everything }

		#if = {
			#not = { has_war_with = POL }

			# POL = { country_event = { id = ausgleich. days = 0 }} 901126
		#}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.40.a

		load_oob = AUS_Ausgleich_war

		add_manpower = 50000

		every_state = {
			limit = { is_core_of = HUN }

			add_core_of = AUS
		}

		every_state = {
			limit = { is_core_of = BOM is_core_of = GAL is_core_of = CRO is_core_of = BOS }

			add_claim_by = AUS
		}
	}
}

	id = ausgleich.41

	desc = ausgleich.41.d

		end_puppet = CRO
		end_puppet = BOM
		end_puppet = GAL
		end_puppet = BOS

		declare_war_on = { target = HUN type = annex_everything }

		#if = {
			#not = { has_war_with = POL }

			# POL = { country_event = { id = ausgleich. days = 0 }} 901126
		#}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.41.a

		load_oob = HUN_Ausgleich_war

		add_manpower = 50000

		hidden_effect = { retire_country_leader = yes remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government }

		create_country_leader = {
			name = "István Bethlen"
			desc = "ISTVAN_BETHLEN_DESC"
			picture = "Portrait_HUN_Istvan_Bethlen.tga"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = paternal_autocratist_subtype
			traits = { }
		}

		add_ideas = HUN_Pal_Teleki_de_Szek_hog_pau

		add_political_power = 100

		HUN = {
			remove_state_core = 644
			remove_state_core = 684
			remove_state_core = 71
			remove_state_core = 73
			remove_state_core = 784

			add_state_claim = 644
			add_state_claim = 684
			add_state_claim = 71
			add_state_claim = 73
			add_state_claim = 784
		}

		CRO = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.42 days = 1 }}
		BOM = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.46 days = 1 }}
		GAL = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.50 days = 1 }}
		BOS = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.59 days = 1 }}
	}

country_event = { # Claim Galicia ?
	id = ausgleich.65
	title = ausgleich.65.t
	desc = ausgleich.65.d
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = POL
		is_puppet = no
		AUS = { has_war_with = HUN }
		country_exists = GAL
		GAL = {
			owns_state = 88
			owns_state = 91
		}
		has_war = no
		NOT = { GAL = { is_puppet_of = POL }}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = galicia_wants_to_join_poland }
		date < 1937.12.29
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.65.a

		ai_chance = { factor = 90 }

		add_state_core = 88
		add_state_core = 91
		add_state_core = 89
		add_state_core = 80

		load_oob = POL_att_GAL

		declare_war_on = { target = GAL type = annex_everything }

		add_opinion_modifier = { target = AUS modifier = POL_att_GAL } # -100
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = HUN modifier = POL_att_GAL } # -100
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = POL_att_GAL_GER } # -20
	}

	option = {
		name = ausgleich.65.b

		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }

		add_opinion_modifier = { target = AUS modifier = POL_no_att_GAL } # 20
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = HUN modifier = POL_no_att_GAL } # 20

		set_global_flag = POL_GAL_bad_idea
	}
}

				is_in_faction_with = GER

			}
		}
	}

		days = 60
	}

	title = ausgleich.106.t
	desc = ausgleich.106.d
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = { 
		tag = AUS
		NOT = {
			has_government = totalist
			has_government = radical_socialist
			has_government = syndicalist
		}
		has_war_with = ROM
		controls_state = 789
		controls_state = 84
		OR = {
			controls_state = 81
			controls_state = 46
		}
		OR = {
			controls_state = 79
			controls_state = 78
		}
		AUS = { is_puppet = no }
		ROM = { is_puppet = no }
		NOT = {
			AUS = {
				is_in_faction_with = FRA
				is_in_faction_with = AUS
				is_in_faction_with = RUS
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.106.a

		ai_chance = { factor = 90 }

		ROM = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.107 }}
		add_state_claim = 81
	}

	option = {
		name = ausgleich.106.b

		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }

		ROM = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.108 }}

	}

		name = ausgleich.106.c

		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }

		add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = AUS_cont_war } # -20
	}
}

#Serbian opportunism

country_event = { # Claim Bosnia?
	id = ausgleich.114
	title = ausgleich.114.t
	desc = ausgleich.114.d
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = { 
		tag = SER
		AUS = { is_puppet = no }
		AUS = { has_war_with = HUN }
		country_exists = BOS
		BOS = { owns_state = 104 }
		has_war = no
		NOT = { BOS = { is_puppet_of = SER }}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = Bosnia_Annexed }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.114.a

		ai_chance = { factor = 90 }

		add_state_core = 104

		load_oob = "SER_war_BOS"

		declare_war_on = {
			target = BOS
			type = take_core_state
			generator = { 104 } 
		}

		add_opinion_modifier = { target = AUS modifier = SER_war_BOS } # -100
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = HUN modifier = SER_war_BOS } # -100
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = SER_war_BOS_GER } # -20
	}

	option = {
		name = ausgleich.114.b

		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }

		add_opinion_modifier = { target = AUS modifier = SER_leaves_BOS } # 20
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = HUN modifier = SER_leaves_BOS } # 20

		set_country_flag = NO_intervention_in_AusCW
	}
}

#  A-H Civil War - German Intervention

country_event = { # Civil War in Austria-Hungary!
	id = ausgleich.126
	title = ausgleich.126.t
	desc = ausgleich.126.d
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = { 
		tag = GER
		NOT = {
			has_government = totalist
			has_government = radical_socialist
			has_government = syndicalist
			GER = {
				has_war_with = AUS
				has_war_with = HUN
				has_war_with = FRA
			}
		}
		AUS = { is_puppet = no }
		AUS = { has_war_with = HUN }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.126.a # Support Austria

		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GERSUP_HUN }
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 35 }

		add_opinion_modifier = { target = AUS modifier = GER_supp_AUS_AUS } # 20
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = HUN modifier = GER_supp_AUS_HUN } # -20
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = GER_supp_AUS } # -5
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = ENG modifier = GER_supp_AUS } # -5
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = ITA modifier = GER_supp_AUS } # -5
		add_manpower = -10000
		AUS = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.127 }}
	}

	option = {
		name = ausgleich.126.b # Support Hungary

		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GERSUP_AUS }
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }

		add_opinion_modifier = { target = AUS modifier = GER_supp_HUN_AUS } # -20
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = HUN modifier = GER_supp_HUN_HUN } # 20
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = GER_supp_HUN } # -5
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = ENG modifier = GER_supp_HUN } # -5
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = ITA modifier = GER_supp_HUN } # -5
		add_manpower = -10000
		HUN = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.128 }}
	}

	option = {
		name = ausgleich.126.c # No Intervention

		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }

		add_opinion_modifier = { target = AUS modifier = GER_no_intervention_AUS } # -20
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = HUN modifier = GER_no_intervention_HUN } # 20
		add_political_power = -40
	}
}

country_event = { # Hungary offers peace
	id = ausgleich.138
	title = ausgleich.138.t
	desc = ausgleich.138.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.138.a

		ai_chance = { factor = 95 }

		white_peace = HUN

		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { 
					country_exists = BOS
					has_war_with = SER
				}
				controls_state = 109
			}

			release = BOS 
			end_puppet = BOS
		}

		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { 
					country_exists = CRO
					has_war_with = CRO
				}
				controls_state = 104
			}

			release = CRO 
			end_puppet = CRO
		}

		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { 
					country_exists = BOM
				}
				controls_state = 9
			}

			release = BOM 
			end_puppet = BOM
		}

		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { 
					country_exists = GAL
					has_war_with = POL
				}
				controls_state = 88
			}

			release = GAL 
			end_puppet = GAL
		}

		end_puppet = POL
		end_puppet = GAL
		end_puppet = BOM
		end_puppet = CRO
		end_puppet = BOS
		end_puppet = ITA
		end_puppet = ROM
		end_puppet = SER
		end_puppet = MTN

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = BOS
				NOT = { BOS = { is_in_faction_with = HUN }}
				NOT = { BOS = { is_in_faction_with = SER }}
			}

			white_peace = BOS 
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = MTN
				NOT = { MTN = { is_in_faction_with = HUN }}
				NOT = { MTN = { is_in_faction_with = SER }}
			}

			white_peace = MTN 
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				HUN = { is_in_faction_with = BOM }
			}

			BOM = {
				transfer_state = 775
			}	
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				HUN = { is_in_faction_with = CRO }
			}

			CRO = {
				transfer_state = 102
				transfer_state = 736
			}	
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					owns_state = 104
					controls_state = 104
				}
			}

			HUN = {
				transfer_state = 104
			}	
		}

		add_timed_idea = { idea = AUS_war_reparations_to_hungary days = 3600 }

		HUN = { add_timed_idea = { idea = AUS_war_reparations_to_hungary_HUN days = 3600 }}

		diplomatic_relation = { country = HUN relation = non_aggression_pact }
	}

	option = {
		name = ausgleich.138.b

		ai_chance = { factor = 5 }

		add_political_power = -140
	}
}

country_event = { # An offer from Austria
	id = ausgleich.152
	title = ausgleich.152.t
	desc = ausgleich.152.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.152.a

		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }

		remove_from_faction = POL

		annex_country = { target = GAL transfer_troops = no }

		every_state = { 
			limit = { is_core_of = GAL } 

			add_core_of = POL
		}

		set_country_flag = Galicia_Annexed

		AUS = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.153 }}

		}

country_event = { # Hungarian demise !
	id = ausgleich.164
	title = ausgleich.164.t
	desc = ausgleich.164.d
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = { 
		tag = AUS
		is_puppet = no
		NOT = {
			has_government = totalist
			has_government = radical_socialist
			has_government = syndicalist
			country_exists = HUN
			has_war_with = BOM
			has_war_with = GAL
			has_war_with = CRO
			has_war_with = BOS
			has_war_with = MTN
			has_war_with = SER
		}
		OR = {
			country_exists = GAL
			country_exists = BOM
			country_exists = CRO
			country_exists = BOS
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.164.a

		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }

		add_state_core = 784
		remove_state_claim = 784

		AUS = {
			transfer_state = 784
		}

		every_state = { 
			limit = { is_core_of = HUN } 

			add_claim_by = AUS
		}

		set_country_flag = hungary_annexed

		add_political_power = 100

		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = BOM
				NOT = { BOM = { has_War_with = AUS }}
				NOT = { BOM = { is_puppet_of = GER }}
				NOT = { BOM = { is_in_faction_with = GER }}
			}

			BOM = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.165 days = 1 }}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = CRO
				NOT = { CRO = { has_War_with = AUS }}
				NOT = { CRO = { is_puppet_of = GER }}
				NOT = { CRO = { is_in_faction_with = GER }}
			}

			CRO = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.166 days = 1 }}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = BOS
				NOT = { BOS = { has_War_with = AUS }}
				NOT = { BOS = { is_puppet_of = GER }}
				NOT = { BOS = { is_in_faction_with = GER }}
			}

			BOS = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.167 days = 1 }}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = GAL
				NOT = { GAL = { has_War_with = AUS }}
				NOT = { GAL = { is_puppet_of = GER }}
				NOT = { GAL = { is_in_faction_with = GER }}
			}

			GAL = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.168 days = 1 }}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ausgleich.164.b

		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

		add_resource = { type = steel amount = 75 state = 152 }
		add_resource = { type = aluminium amount = 10 state = 152 }
		add_resource = { type = steel amount = 75 state = 9 }
		add_resource = { type = tungsten amount = 20 state = 70 }

		set_global_flag = AH_Cabinet_yes

		set_country_flag = aus_178
	}
}

country_event = { # Establishment of the Danubian Federation
	id = ausgleich.179
	title = ausgleich.179.t
	desc = ausgleich.179.d
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = { 
		tag = AUS
		has_global_flag = AUS_Danube_yes
		NOT = { has_global_flag = aus_175_b has_global_flag = aus_175_a }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.179.a

		DNF = { transfer_state = 4 }

		every_state = { 
			limit = { is_core_of = AUS } 

			add_core_of = DNF
		}

		every_state = { 
			limit = { is_claimed_by = AUS } 

			add_claim_by = DNF
		}

		DNF = { change_tag_from = AUS }

		DNF = { annex_country = { target = AUS transfer_troops = yes }}

		DNF = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.180 days = 1 }}
		hidden_effect = { DNF = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.231 days = 0 }}}
		hidden_effect = { DNF = { country_event = { id = focus.1 days = 0 }}}

		clr_global_flag = AUS_Danube_yes

		set_country_flag = DNF_For

		add_political_power = -300	
	}
}

country_event = { # Reorganisation of the Federation
	id = ausgleich.180
	title = ausgleich.180.t
	desc = ausgleich.180.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.180.a

		if = {
			limit = {
				controls_state = 105
			}

			add_state_core = 105
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				controls_state = 160
			}

			add_state_core = 160
		}

		every_state = { 
			limit = { is_claimed_by = AUS } 

			add_core_of = DNF
		}

		add_popularity = {
            ideology = social_conservatist
            popularity = 0.2
        }

        set_politics = { ruling_party = social_conservatist elections_allowed = no }

        hidden_effect = { retire_country_leader = yes }

        create_country_leader = {
			name = "S.K.u.K.M. Otto I von Habsburg"
			desc = "POLITICS_OTTO_DESC"
			picture = "Portrait_Austria_Otto_I_2.tga"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = social_conservatist_subtype
			traits = { }
		}

		add_manpower = 200000

		load_oob = "DNF"

		set_country_flag = aus_180

		DNF = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.181 days = 1 }}
	}
}

country_event = { # Choosing the sides
	id = ausgleich.189
	title = ausgleich.189.t
	desc = ausgleich.189.d
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = { 
		tag = AHE
		has_country_flag = AUS_HUN_For
		is_puppet = no
		has_war = no
		NOT = { 
			is_in_faction_with = CAN
			is_in_faction_with = GER
			is_in_faction_with = RUS
			is_in_faction_with = JAP
			is_in_faction_with = FRA
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 200 }
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.189.a # Canada

		trigger = {
			country_exists = CAN
			CAN = { is_puppet = no }
			NOT = {
				has_government = totalist
				has_government = radical_socialist
				has_government = syndicalist
			}
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }

		CAN = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.194 days = 1 }}
	}

	option = {
		name = ausgleich.189.b # Germany

		trigger = {
			country_exists = GER
			GER = { is_puppet = no }
			NOT = {
				has_government = totalist
				has_government = radical_socialist
				has_government = syndicalist
			}
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 45 }

		AHE = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.197 days = 1 }}
	}

	option = {
		name = ausgleich.189.c # France

		trigger = {
			country_exists = FRA
			FRA = { is_puppet = no }
			has_government = totalist
			has_government = radical_socialist
			has_government = syndicalist
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 15 }

		AHE = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.203 days = 1 }}
	}

	option = {
		name = ausgleich.189.e # New Bloc

		trigger = {
			country_exists = RUS
			NOT = {
				has_government = totalist
				has_government = radical_socialist
				has_government = syndicalist
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					POL = { is_puppet = no }
					NOT = { is_in_faction_with = POL }
				}
				AND = {
					RUS = { is_puppet = no }
					RUS = {
						controls_state = 195
						controls_state = 219
						controls_state = 583
						controls_state = 566
						controls_state = 562
					}
					NOT = {
						RUS = {
							is_in_faction_with = CAN
							is_in_faction_with = NFA
							is_in_faction_with = GER
							is_in_faction_with = JAP
							is_in_faction_with = CHI
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }

		AHE = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.207 days = 1 }}
	}

	option = {
		name = ausgleich.189.f

		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }

		add_political_power = 200
	}
}

	id = ausgleich.191
	title = ausgleich.191.t
	desc = ausgleich.191.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.191.a # YES

		ai_chance = { factor = 94 }

		CAN = { add_to_faction = DNF }
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = DNF modifier = DNF_ally_CAN } # 100
		add_political_power = 60
		DNF = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.193 days = 1 }}
	}

	option = {
		name = ausgleich.191.b # NO

		ai_chance = { factor = 5 }

		add_political_power = -20
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = DNF modifier = DNF_no_ally_CAN } # -100
	}

	option = {
		name = ausgleich.191.c # NAP ?

		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }

		DNF = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.196 days = 1 }}
		add_political_power = -20
	}

country_event = { # Austria-Hungary wants to form new block
	id = ausgleich.213
	title = ausgleich.213.t
	desc = ausgleich.213.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.213.a # YES

		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }

		add_opinion_modifier = { target = AHE modifier = AHE_ally_POL } # 100
		add_political_power = 140
		AHE = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.214 days = 1 }}
	}

	option = {
		name = ausgleich.213.b # Exchange Galicia

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					AHE = { 
						controls_state = 88
						controls_state = 91
					}
					NOT = {
						country_exists = GAL
					}	
				}
				AND = {
					country_exists = GAL
					NOT = { GAL = { is_puppet_of = POL }}
					GAL = {
						controls_state = 88
						controls_state = 91
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 90 }

		every_state = {
			limit = { is_core_of = GAL }

			add_core_of = POL
		}

		AHE = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.219 days = 1 }}
	}

	option = {
		name = ausgleich.213.c # NO

		ai_chance = { factor = 5 }

		add_political_power = -20
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = AHE modifier = AHE_no_ally_POL } # -100
	}
}

country_event = { # New power in Europe
	id = ausgleich.214
	title = ausgleich.214.t
	desc = ausgleich.214.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.214.a
	
		add_political_power = 60

		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = no
			}

			create_faction = "Central Powers"
		}

		AHE = { add_to_faction = POL }
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = POL modifier = POL_ally_AHE } # 200
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = AHE_ally_POL_FRA } # -150
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = AHE_ally_POL_GER } # -70
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = embargo }
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = embargo }
	}
}

country_event = { # The Polish Answer
	id = ausgleich.217
	title = ausgleich.217.t
	desc = ausgleich.217.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.217.a # YES

		ai_chance = { factor = 80 }

		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = no
			}

			create_faction = "Central Powers"
		}

		DNF = { add_to_faction = POL }

		add_opinion_modifier = { target = POL modifier = DNF_ally_POL } # 200

		POL = {
			transfer_state = 88
			transfer_state = 91
			transfer_state = 89
			transfer_state = 80
		}

		DNF = {
			remove_state_core = 88
			remove_state_core = 91
			remove_state_core = 89
			remove_state_core = 80
		}

		POL = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.218 days = 1 }}
	}

	option = {
		name = ausgleich.217.b # NO

		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }

		add_political_power = -20
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = DNF modifier = DNF_no_ally_POL } # -200
	}
}

#########################################################################
#  A-H Civil War - Russian Intervention
#########################################################################

country_event = { # Civil War in Austria-Hungary!
	id = ausgleich.221
	title = ausgleich.221.t
	desc = ausgleich.221.d
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = { 
		tag = RUS
		AUS = { has_war_with = HUN }
		NOT = {
			RUS = {
				has_war_With = AUS
				has_war_With = HUN
				has_country_flag = RUS_ISO
				has_global_flag = RUS_ISO
			}
			country_exists = SOV
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					country_exists = UKR
					RUS = { controls_state = 202 }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				country_exists = UKR
				UKR = { controls_state = 202 }
				OR = {
					UKR = { is_in_faction_with = RUS }
					UKR = { is_puppet_of = RUS }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.221.a # Support Austria

		ai_chance = { factor = 35 }

		add_opinion_modifier = { target = AUS modifier = RUS_supp_AUS_AUS } # 20
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = HUN modifier = RUS_supp_AUS_HUN } # -20
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = RUS_supp_AUS } # -5
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = ENG modifier = RUS_supp_AUS } # -5
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = ITA modifier = RUS_supp_AUS } # -5
		add_manpower = -10000
		AUS = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.222 }}
	}

	option = {
		name = ausgleich.221.b # Support Hungary

		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }

		add_opinion_modifier = { target = AUS modifier = RUS_supp_HUN_AUS } # -20
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = HUN modifier = RUS_supp_HUN_HUN } # 20
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = RUS_supp_HUN } # -5
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = ENG modifier = RUS_supp_HUN } # -5
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = ITA modifier = RUS_supp_HUN } # -5
		add_manpower = -10000
		HUN = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.223 }}
	}

	option = {
		name = ausgleich.221.c # No Intervention

		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }

		add_opinion_modifier = { target = AUS modifier = RUS_no_intervention_AUS } # -20
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = HUN modifier = RUS_no_intervention_HUN } # 20
		add_political_power = -40
	}
}

#### 1947/1957 Ausgleich

country_event = { # 1947 Ausgleich
	id = ausgleich.227
	title = ausgleich.227.t
	desc = ausgleich.227.d
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = { 
		tag = AHE
		is_puppet = no
		NOT = {
			has_government = totalist
			has_government = radical_socialist
			has_government = syndicalist
		}
		date > 1947.2.15
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ausgleich.227.a

		ai_chance = { factor = 75 }

		add_political_power = -60
	}

	option = {
		name = ausgleich.227.b

		ai_chance = { factor = 24 }

		add_political_power = -100

		add_popularity = {
            ideology = social_conservatist
            popularity = 0.1
        }
	}

	option = {
		name = ausgleich.227.c

		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }

		DNF = { transfer_state = 4 }

		every_state = { 
			limit = { is_core_of = AHE } 

			add_core_of = DNF
		}

		every_state = { 
			limit = { is_claimed_by = AHE } 

			add_claim_by = DNF
		}

		DNF = { change_tag_from = AUS }

		DNF = { annex_country = { target = AHE transfer_troops = yes }}

		DNF = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.180 days = 1 }}
		hidden_effect = { DNF = { country_event = { id = ausgleich.231 days = 0 }}}
		hidden_effect = { DNF = { country_event = { id = focus.1 days = 0 }}}

		add_political_power = -300	

		add_popularity = {
            ideology = social_conservatist
            popularity = 0.2
        }

		set_politics = { ruling_party = social_conservatist elections_allowed = no }

		hidden_effect = { 
			retire_country_leader = yes

			remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
		}

		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Otto I von Habsburg-Lothringen"
			desc = "POLITICS_OTTO_DESC"
			picture = "Portrait_Austria_Otto_I_2.tga"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = social_conservatist_subtype
			traits = { }
		}

		set_global_flag = danubian_federation
	}
}
